<p><br/>
The following is a list of <b>notable deaths in April 2015</b>.</p>
<p>Entries for each day are listed <u>alphabetically</u> by surname. A typical entry lists information in the following sequence:</p>
<ul>
<li>Name, age, country of citizenship and reason for notability, established cause of death, reference.</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="April_2015">April 2015</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Deaths_in_April_2015&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: April 2015">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1"><a href="/wiki/April_1" title="April 1">1</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Deaths_in_April_2015&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dave_Ball_(musician)" title="Dave Ball (musician)">Dave Ball</a>, 65, British musician (<a href="/wiki/Procol_Harum" title="Procol Harum">Procol Harum</a>), colorectal cancer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Roel_Cortez" title="Roel Cortez">Roel Cortez</a>, 47, Filipino singer-songwriter, colon cancer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Peter_Diamandopoulos" title="Peter Diamandopoulos">Peter Diamandopoulos</a>, 86, Greek-born American academic, President of <a href="/wiki/Adelphi_University" title="Adelphi University">Adelphi University</a> (1985–1997).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Johnny_Gardiner" title="Johnny Gardiner">Johnny Gardiner</a>, 92, Canadian <a href="/wiki/Canadian_Football_League" title="Canadian Football League">CFL</a> football player (<a href="/wiki/Winnipeg_Blue_Bombers" title="Winnipeg Blue Bombers">Winnipeg Blue Bombers</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/John_Paul_Hammerschmidt" title="John Paul Hammerschmidt">John Paul Hammerschmidt</a>, 92, American politician, member of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">US House of Representatives</a> from <a href="/wiki/Arkansas" title="Arkansas">Arkansas</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Arkansas%27s_3rd_congressional_district" title="Arkansas's 3rd congressional district">3rd district</a> (1967–1993), heart and respiratory failure.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/John_Ingram_(engineer)" title="John Ingram (engineer)">Sir John Ingram</a>, 90, New Zealand engineer and businessman.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Zdravko-%C4%86iro_Kova%C4%8Di%C4%87" title="Zdravko-Ćiro Kovačić">Zdravko-Ćiro Kovačić</a>, 89, Croatian water polo player, Olympic silver medalist for Yugoslavia (<a href="/wiki/Water_polo_at_the_1952_Summer_Olympics" title="Water polo at the 1952 Summer Olympics">1952</a>, <a href="/wiki/Water_polo_at_the_1956_Summer_Olympics" title="Water polo at the 1956 Summer Olympics">1956</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Eddie_LeBaron" title="Eddie LeBaron">Eddie LeBaron</a>, 85, American football player (<a href="/wiki/Washington_Redskins" title="Washington Redskins">Washington Redskins</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dallas_Cowboys" title="Dallas Cowboys">Dallas Cowboys</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cynthia_Lennon" title="Cynthia Lennon">Cynthia Lennon</a>, 75, British author, cancer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Raul_Loya" title="Raul Loya">Raul Loya</a>, 76, American workers' rights activist.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Misao_Okawa" title="Misao Okawa">Misao Okawa</a>, 117, Japanese supercentenarian, world's oldest living person, heart failure.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nicolae_Rainea" title="Nicolae Rainea">Nicolae Rainea</a>, 81, Romanian football referee (<a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">FIFA World Cup</a> (<a href="/wiki/1974_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1974 FIFA World Cup">1974</a>, <a href="/wiki/1978_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1978 FIFA World Cup">1978</a>, <a href="/wiki/1982_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1982 FIFA World Cup">1982</a>), <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_1980_Final" title="UEFA Euro 1980 Final">UEFA Euro 1980 Final</a>), pulmonary edema.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Roy_Ralph" title="Roy Ralph">Roy Ralph</a>, 94, English cricketer (<a href="/wiki/Essex_County_Cricket_Club" title="Essex County Cricket Club">Essex</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Paul_D._Reynolds" title="Paul D. Reynolds">Paul D. Reynolds</a>, 52, Canadian investment banker, CEO of <a href="/wiki/Canaccord_Genuity" title="Canaccord Genuity">Canaccord Genuity</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/J._D._Smith_(fullback,_born_1931)" title="J. D. Smith (fullback, born 1931)">J. D. Smith</a>, 83, American football player (<a href="/wiki/San_Francisco_49ers" title="San Francisco 49ers">San Francisco 49ers</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Joseph_Sweda" title="Joseph Sweda">Joseph Sweda</a>, 89, American politician.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Robert_Walker_(animator)" title="Robert Walker (animator)">Robert Walker</a>, 54, Canadian-born American animator and director (<i><a href="/wiki/Aladdin_(1992_Disney_film)" title="Aladdin (1992 Disney film)">Aladdin</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Brother_Bear" title="Brother Bear">Brother Bear</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Mulan_(1998_film)" title="Mulan (1998 film)">Mulan</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Lion_King" title="The Lion King">The Lion King</a></i>), heart attack.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Muhammadu_Dikko_Yusufu" title="Muhammadu Dikko Yusufu">Muhammadu Dikko Yusufu</a>, 84, Nigerian politician and police officer, Inspector General of the Police (1976–1979).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2"><a href="/wiki/April_2" title="April 2">2</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Deaths_in_April_2015&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Paule_Anglim" title="Paule Anglim">Paule Anglim</a>, 92, Canadian-born American art dealer (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gallery_Paule_Anglim" title="Gallery Paule Anglim">Gallery Paule Anglim</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Luis_Delgado_Aparicio" title="Luis Delgado Aparicio">Luis Delgado Aparicio</a>, 74, Peruvian politician, <a href="/wiki/Congress_of_the_Republic_of_Peru" title="Congress of the Republic of Peru">MP</a> (1995–2001), pancreatic cancer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Natalia_Bobrova" title="Natalia Bobrova">Natalia Bobrova</a>, 36, Russian gymnast, stomach cancer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mick_Brown_(judge)" title="Mick Brown (judge)">Mick Brown</a>, 77, New Zealand jurist.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Per_Vilhelm_Br%C3%BCel" title="Per Vilhelm Brüel">Per Vilhelm Brüel</a>, 100, Danish engineer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wally_Cassell" title="Wally Cassell">Wally Cassell</a>, 103, Italian-born American actor (<i><a href="/wiki/White_Heat" title="White Heat">White Heat</a></i>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tom_Coyne_(broadcaster)" title="Tom Coyne (broadcaster)">Tom Coyne</a>, 84, British news broadcaster and television presenter (<i><a href="/wiki/Top_Gear_(1977_TV_series)" title="Top Gear (1977 TV series)">Top Gear</a></i>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25"><a href="#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/James_de_Beaujeu_Domville" title="James de Beaujeu Domville">James de Beaujeu Domville</a>, 81, French-born Canadian theatrical producer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/William_Benedict_Friend" title="William Benedict Friend">William Benedict Friend</a>, 83, American Roman Catholic prelate, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Alexandria_in_Louisiana" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Alexandria in Louisiana">Alexandria-Shreveport</a> (1982–1986) and <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Shreveport" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Shreveport">Shreveport</a> (1986–2006).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ra%C3%BAl_Gorriti" title="Raúl Gorriti">Raúl Gorriti</a>, 58, Peruvian footballer (<a href="/wiki/Peru_national_football_team" title="Peru national football team">national team</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Robert_Blair_Kaiser" title="Robert Blair Kaiser">Robert Blair Kaiser</a>, 84, American journalist.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29"><a href="#cite_note-29">[29]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dennis_Marks_(music_director)" title="Dennis Marks (music director)">Dennis Marks</a>, 66, British television producer and music director.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ben_Meisner" title="Ben Meisner">Ben Meisner</a>, 76, Canadian broadcaster (<a href="/wiki/CKPG-TV" title="CKPG-TV">CKPG</a>), cancer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Norman_H._Nie" title="Norman H. Nie">Norman H. Nie</a>, 72, American social scientist, lung cancer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hayley_Okines" title="Hayley Okines">Hayley Okines</a>, 17, British <a href="/wiki/Progeria" title="Progeria">progeria</a> campaigner, pneumonia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Manoel_de_Oliveira" title="Manoel de Oliveira">Manoel de Oliveira</a>, 106, Portuguese film director and screenwriter, heart failure.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Stanis%C5%82aw_Pestka" title="Stanisław Pestka">Stanisław Pestka</a>, 85, Polish <a href="/wiki/Kashubians" title="Kashubians">Kashubian</a> poet.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Joseph_L._Reid_(oceanographer)" title="Joseph L. Reid (oceanographer)">Joseph L. Reid</a>, 92, American oceanographer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36"><a href="#cite_note-36">[36]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Barbara_Sass" title="Barbara Sass">Barbara Sass</a>, 78, Polish film director and screenwriter.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Olga_Sawicka" title="Olga Sawicka">Olga Sawicka</a>, 83, Polish dancer and choreographer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Doug_Sax" title="Doug Sax">Doug Sax</a>, 79, American audio mastering engineer, cancer.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39"><a href="#cite_note-39">[39]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Robert_H._Schuller" title="Robert H. Schuller">Robert H. Schuller</a>, 88, American televangelist (<i><a href="/wiki/Hour_of_Power" title="Hour of Power">Hour of Power</a></i>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Alberto_Ricardo_da_Silva" title="Alberto Ricardo da Silva">Alberto Ricardo da Silva</a>, 71, East Timorese Roman Catholic prelate, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_D%C3%ADli" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Díli">Díli</a> (2004–2015).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Steve_Stevaert" title="Steve Stevaert">Steve Stevaert</a>, 60, Belgian politician, Chairman of the <a href="/wiki/Socialistische_Partij_Anders" title="Socialistische Partij Anders">SP.a</a> (2003–2005), Governor of <a href="/wiki/Limburg_(Belgium)" title="Limburg (Belgium)">Limburg</a> (2005–2009).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/David_Fonseca_(politician)" title="David Fonseca (politician)">David Fonseca</a>, 60, Belizean politician, Mayor of <a href="/wiki/Belize_City" title="Belize City">Belize City</a> (1999–2006), suicide by gunshot.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-564"><a href="#cite_note-564">[564]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Adrian_Gibson" title="Adrian Gibson">Adrian Gibson</a>, 79, Australian politician, MP for <a href="/wiki/Division_of_Denison" title="Division of Denison">Denison</a> (1964–69).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-565"><a href="#cite_note-565">[565]</a></sup></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Rutger_Gunnarsson" title="Rutger Gunnarsson">Rutger Gunnarsson</a>, 69, Swedish bassist (<a href="/wiki/ABBA" title="ABBA">ABBA</a>, <a href="/wiki/Elton_John" title="Elton John">Elton John</a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-567"><a href="#cite_note-567">[567]</a></sup></li>

</ul>
